 varsh 2016 main papamochani ekadshi vrath 4 april ke din kiya jaayegaa
 According to mythological beliefs, Ekadashi of Chaitra Krishna Paksha is supposed to destroy sins
 swayan bhagwaan shri krishna ne iske fal evam prabhaav ko arjuna ke samaksh prastut kiya tha
 The Papamochani Ekadashi fast opens the path of salvation for the seeker by ridding him of all his sins
 is ekadshi ke din bhagwaan vishnu ji kaa pujan karnaa chahie
 If a person performs this pooja with complete law and practice, the auspicious results of the fast increase
 papamochani ekadshi kii kathakatha ke anusaar bhagwaan arjuna se kehete hai, raja mandhata ne ek samay main lomash rishi se jab poocha ki prabhu yah bataaen ki manushya jo jane anjaane paap karm karata he usase kaise mukt ho saktaa he
 In response to King Mandhata's question, the Lomash sage told a story to the king that in the beautiful forest called Chaitratha, the meritorious sage, son of Chyavan Rishi, was absorbed in penance
 is van main ek din manjughosha naamak apsara kii nazar rishi par padi to vah un par mohit ho gayi or unhen apni ore aakarshith karne hetu ytn karne lagi
 Kamdev was also passing by at that time that his eyes went to Apsara and he understood her feelings and started helping her
 apsara apane ytn main safal hui or rishi kampidit ho gaye
 The sage forgot the fast of penance of Shiva and started Ramana with Apsara
 kai varshon ke baad jab unki chetana jaagi to unhen ehsaas hua ki vah shiv kii tapasya se virat ho chuke hai
 He was very angry at the nymph and, guilty of breaking austerities, the sage cursed the nymph to be a vampire
 shraap se dukhi hokar vah rishi ke pairon par gir padi or shraap se mukti ke liye anunay karne lagi
 The meritorious sage, who was moved by the plea of apsara, asked him to observe Chaitra Krishna Ekadashi with the method, because of being immersed in the enjoyment, the sage's glory was also lost
 isliye rishi ne bhi is ekadshi kaa vrath kiya jisase unka paap nasht ho gaya
 On the other hand, Apsara was also freed from the vampire vagina by the effect of this fast and she got a beautiful form and departed for heaven
 paap mochani ekadshi pujan vidhi- is vrath main bhagwaan vishnu ke chaturbhuj rup kii puja kii jaati he
 Vrati should eat sattvic food once on Dashami Tithi and should offer prayers to Lord Vishnu by removing the feeling of enjoyment from the mind
 - ekadshi ke din suryoday hote hi snaan karke vrath kaa sankalp karnaa chahie sankalp ke uparant shri vishnu kii puja karen
 - After worship, one should recite or listen to Bhagwad Katha before sitting in front of God
 - ekadshi tithi ko jaagran karne se kai guna punya miltaa he

 garmiyon kaa mausam apane saath skin kii kai samasyaon ko saath lekar aata he
 The scorching heat of summer and hot winds damage the skin badly
 garmi kaa mausam shuru hote hi kai logon main pigmentation, san bern, rashes kii samasya aam ho jaati he
 People whose skin is sensitive, their skin gets scorched due to excessive heat and the color also starts turning black
 ham aapako kuch tips bataa rahe hai, jinhen follow kar ke aap skin sambandhit kai samasyaon se batch sakate hai
 1
 munhaase-garmi ke mausam main zyada pasinaa aane se skin ke porce main tel or bacteria jamaa hone lagate hai, jisase munhaase nikalne lagate hai
 According to the American Academy of Dermatology, most people around the world suffer from acne and rash problems
 isse bachane ke liye jaruri he ki aap din main do baar chehre ko thande pani se jarur dhoen
 2
 dry skin-garmi ke mausam main zyada pasinaa aane, A
 The skin becomes dry due to sitting in the c room and staying in the swimming pool for a long time
 american academy of dermatology ke mutabik, dry skin kii samasya se bachane ke liye niyamit taur par moischarizer kaa istemaal jarur karen
 To avoid dryness, use mild face wash and mild soap only
 3
 Skin allergy - Many people get skin allergy due to exposure to sunlight
 skin par laal chakatte padane lagate hai, jinamein khujali bhi hoti he
 To avoid this, avoid going in the sun as much as possible
 jab bhi baahar jaaen khud ko acchhee tarah se cover jarur kar len
 Be sure to contact the doctor if you are very allergic
 4
 Sunburn - As soon as the summer season starts, most people start to suffer from sunburn
 sanbern se bachane ke liye dhoop main nikalne se pehle sanscreen jarur lagaaein
 Let me tell you, the effect of sunscreen lasts only for two hours
 isliye dhoop main nikalate vakt is baat kaa dhyaan jarur rakhen
 While going out in summer, wear only such clothes, so that the body is completely covered
